# Atlassian (atlassian)

Atlassian is a software company that develops collaboration, productivity, and project management tools to help teams work more efficiently. Its products are designed to enhance teamwork, streamline workflows, and support project tracking across a wide range of industries.

**APIs.json:** [https://raw.githubusercontent.com/api-evangelist/atlassian/refs/heads/main/apis.yml](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/api-evangelist/atlassian/refs/heads/main/apis.yml)

## Scope

- **Position:** Consuming
- **Access:** 3rd-Party

## Tags

- Code
- Collaboration
- Platform
- Productivity
- Software Development

## Timestamps

- **Created:** 2024-04-14
- **Modified:** 2026-05-19

## APIs

### Atlassian Bitbucket Addon API

The Atlassian Bitbucket Addon API allows developers to create custom add-ons and integrations for the Bitbucket platform, extending functionality with new features, tools, and services.

- **Human URL:** [https://developer.atlassian.com/cloud/bitbucket/rest/api-group-addon/#api-group-addon](https://developer.atlassian.com/cloud/bitbucket/rest/api-group-addon/#api-group-addon)

#### Tags

- Addons
- Applications
- Bitbucket

#### Properties

- [OpenAPI](openapi/atlassian-addon--openapi-original.yml) — [OpenAPI Specification](https://spec.openapis.org/oas/latest.html)
- [Documentation](https://developer.atlassian.com/cloud/bitbucket/rest/api-group-addon/)

### Atlassian Bitbucket Hook Events API

The Atlassian Bitbucket Hook Events API enables users to create webhooks in Bitbucket repositories to trigger custom actions whenever specific events occur.

- **Human URL:** [https://developer.atlassian.com/cloud/bitbucket/rest/api-group-webhooks/#api-group-webhooks](https://developer.atlassian.com/cloud/bitbucket/rest/api-group-webhooks/#api-group-webhooks)

#### Tags

- Bitbucket
- Events
- Webhooks

#### Properties

- [OpenAPI](openapi/atlassian-hook-events--openapi-original.yml) — [OpenAPI Specification](https://spec.openapis.org/oas/latest.html)
- [Documentation](https://developer.atlassian.com/cloud/bitbucket/rest/api-group-webhooks/)
- [JSON-LD](json-ld/atlassian-bitbucket-hook-events-context.jsonld) — [JSON-LD](https://www.w3.org/TR/json-ld11/)
- [JSON Schema](json-schema/atlassian-bitbucket-hook-events-paginated_hook_events-schema.json) — [JSON Schema](https://json-schema.org/specification)

### Atlassian Bitbucket Pull Requests API

The Atlassian Bitbucket Pull Requests API allows users to interact with pull requests in their repositories, providing endpoints for viewing, creating, updating, and merging pull requests.

- **Human URL:** [https://developer.atlassian.com/cloud/bitbucket/rest/api-group-pullrequests/#api-group-pullrequests](https://developer.atlassian.com/cloud/bitbucket/rest/api-group-pullrequests/#api-group-pullrequests)

- Pull Requests

- **Human URL:** [https://developer.atlassian.com/cloud/bitbucket/rest/api-group-branch-restrictions/#api-group-branch-restrictions](https://developer.atlassian.com/cloud/bitbucket/rest/api-group-branch-restrictions/#api-group-branch-restrictions)

### Atlassian Bitbucket Reports API

- **Human URL:** [https://developer.atlassian.com/cloud/bitbucket/rest/api-group-reports/#api-group-reports](https://developer.atlassian.com/cloud/bitbucket/rest/api-group-reports/#api-group-reports)
